Bicolor 2048

2048, but tiles come in two colors, and they can only merge if they're opposite colors. The color of the resulting tile is the color of the tile being collided into.

Suggested by Michael Darrow, created by MathCookie

Harder 2584

Merges occur between two equal tiles and one of the tile before them, or between three 1s. The resulting tile is two tiles later than the equal tiles.

Created by Michael Darrow

1822

If a tile is a multiple of 3, it merges with a 1. If a tile is 1 more than a multiple of 3, it merges with a tile that's equal to itself. If a tile is 2 more than a multiple of 3, it merges with a tile that's half of itself.

Created by Michael Darrow

Alternating Merge Sets 2048

2048, but tiles come in two colors, red and green. After each turn, all tiles swap their color. Two tiles can only merge if they're both currently green.

2048... but with obstacles

Two equal tiles merge. There are junk tiles which can be destroyed by moving two tiles that are about to merge onto it.

Created by Toni Brown

12TET

n + n = 2n, n + 2n = 3n, 2n + 3n = 5n. This is approximated using 12-tone temperament. At higher numbers, close enough numbers may end up acting as the same tile.

Created by Michael Darrow

22TET

n + n = 2n, n + 2n = 3n, 2n + 3n = 5n, 2n + 5n = 7n, 4n + 7n = 11n. This is approximated using 22-tone temperament. At higher numbers, close enough numbers may end up acting as the same tile.

Bohlen Pierce

n + n + n = 3n, n + n + 3n = 5n, n + 3n + 3n = 7n, n + n + 5n = 7n. This is approximated using the Bohlen-Pierce scale, which is a 13-tone 3:1 temperament. At higher numbers, close enough numbers may end up acting as the same tile.

Created by Michael Darrow

Powers of 14

2744

Merges occur between three equal tiles that are a power of 14, between a tile that's a power of 14 and two tiles that are triple that power of 14, or between two equal tiles that are seven times a power of 14.

Created by aren12345

3024

1 is the 1st tile. The 1st, 3rd, 5th, 7th, and so on tiles merge with an equal tile. The 2nd, 6th, 10th, 14th, and so on tiles merge with the previous tile. The 4th, 12th, 20th, 28th, and so on tiles merge with the tile two tiles before it. In general, if a tile's index is a multiple of 2^n but not of 2^(n + 1), then it merges with the tile n tiles before it.

Created by MathCookie

1807

Similar to 3024. If a tile's index is a multiple of 2^n but not of 2^(n + 1), then it merges with the tile (2^n) - 1 tiles before it.

Created by Michael Darrow

5832

Positive and Negative Powers of 3

±243

Two equal tiles that are equal to one, negative one, two, or negative two times a power of three can merge. A tile that is four times or negative four times a power of three merges with a tile that is negative one-fourth of it.

1970

Two 1s can merge. Larger tiles merge with the largest odd tile under them.

2018

Two 1s can merge. Tiles merge with the largest tile less than them that is 1 modulo 3.

Powers of 45

2025

Three equal tiles can merge if they are a power of 45. A tile that's a power of 45, triple a power of 45, or nine times a power of 45 can merge with a tile equal to itself and a tile triple itself. A tile that's a power of 45 or triple a power of 45 can merge with a tile triple itself and a tile quintuple itself.

Created by MathCookie

Quadronacci Sequence (like Tetranacci, but starting with four 1s)

2500

Quadronacci is a sequence Q_n that satisfies Q_n=Q_(n-1)+Q_(n-2)+Q_(n-3)+Q_(n-4). A Q_n and a Q_(n-1) can merge (n can be any number),A (Q_n+Q_(n-1)) and a (Q_(n-2)+Q_(n-3)) can merge. Q_1~Q_4 are all 1.

Created by aren12345

Interleaved 2187

Two 1s can merge into a 2, and a 1 and a 2 can merge into a 3. Merges occur between a tile that's three times a power of three and a tile that's one, two, or three times that power of three, or between a tile that's four times a power of three and a tile that's five times that power of three.

Powers of 2 Times Fibonacci Numbers

2059

This mode uses the F_-1 = 0 convention for Fibonacci numbers. Merges may occur between two equal 2^n * F_n tiles, or between a 2^(n+1) * F_n tile and two 2^n * F_(n-1) tiles.

Created by Michael Darrow

22edo Powers of 2 Times Powers of 3 Times Powers of 5

Any two 5-smooth tiles may merge if their result is also 5-smooth. This is approximated using 22-tone temperament. At higher numbers, close enough numbers may end up acting as the same tile.

3855

A tile that is divisible by 2^2^n - 1 but not by 2^2^(n + 1) - 1 merges with two tiles that are a (2^2^n - 1)th of it.

Created by Michael Darrow

1640 1641

Merges occur between three equal throdd tiles, or between two equal throdd tiles and a threeven tile that is one away from them.

Created by Michael Darrow

Interleaved 2187

Three 1s can merge into a 3, and three 3s can merge into a 9. A merge occurs between a tile that's a power of three, a tile that's triple that power of three, and a tile that's nine times that power of three, or between a tile that's a power of three and two tiles that are thirteen times that power of three.

Suggested by Michael Darrow, created by MathCookie

Mersenne Numbers And Fermat Numbers

2047 2049

Three 1s merge into a 3. Two unequal tiles that are one away from the same power of two can merge with a 1 or -1.

RGB 2304

The tiles in this mode come in RGB colors. Two tiles of the same tier that are different primary colors can merge. A secondary color tile can merge with its complementary color tile of the same tier. A white tile can merge with any primary color tile of its tier, creating that primary color tile of the next tier.

Created by MathCookie

Powers of 16

Harder 4096

Merges occur between three equal tiles that are a power of 16, between two or three tiles that are triple a power of 16, between a tile that's a power of 16 and a tile that's nine times that power of 16, or between a tile that's six times a power of 16 and a tile that's ten times that power of 16.

Created by marouane

(2n+1)*2^(2n+1)

4608

Two equal tiles can merge if they are a power of 2 or if they are of the form (2n+1)*2^k, where k is 2n-1 or 2n. A (2n-1)*2^(2n-1) tile can merge with a 2^2n tile.

Created by aren12345

3072 5120

Two 1s merge into a 2. 1 and 2 are considered the first "tier" of tiles. A tile on tier n merges with a tile whose difference with it is 2^(n - 1).

Created by MathCookie

Interleaved 2187: TRIGAT variant

Two 1s merge into a 2,a 2 and a 1 merge into a 3.A power of three can merge with a tile that is 2/3 of it, a 5/3 times power of three can merge with a tile that is 1/5 of it, a 2 times power of three can merge with a tile that is half of it.

Padovan's sequence

2513

The first three terms of Padovan's sequence are all 1, merge occur between a tile and the tile before it, but the result tile is the tile two after it.

1562 1563

Square Numbers

361

Two 1s merge into a 2. An odd number merges with 2 into the next odd number. A square number merges with an odd number into the next square number. (In the case of odd squares like 9 and 25, the square number and the odd number are two different tiles with the same number)

Originally created by Toni Brown, polished by MathCookie

Fueling 2048

Two equal tiles merge, but when a new tile spawns or is made, it starts out "inactive" (unable to merge), and must merge with a fuel 0 first to become active.

Created by MathCookie

Show Save Code

Divisors of 2520

2520 (2-Tile Merges)

Two tiles merge if their sum is a divisor of 2520.

Highly Composite Numbers

2520

Tiles are highly composite numbers, and a given tile merges with one or two smaller tiles (one if possible, two only if one is not possible) to make the next HCN.

Reverse 2584

Merges occur between any tile and the tile before it, but the first two tiles are -2584 and 1597, and your goal is to make a 1.

Originally created by aren12345, polished by MathCookie

Pythagorean Triples

4059, 4060, 5741

Three tiles that make up a Pythagorean triple merge. A tile that's the sum of a Pythagorean triple merges with two tiles, one of which is the largest tile of that triple and the other of which is either one of the other two tiles of that triple or another copy of the triple's sum.

Created by aren12345
